msg:First, let‚Äôs talk about what makes you satisfied
1. The aunts who clean the rooms in the housekeeping department are very polite when they see the guests. When they saw that I had a lot of luggage, they helped me carry it and pressed the elevator. They were very kind.
2. Breakfast includes freshly made noodles and freshly ground soy milk. Generally speaking, it is quite rich and tastes good.
3. The location is good. Downstairs are Ma Wangzi and Granny Ye, as well as a milk tea shop. Opposite are Taikoo Li's Cuiyuan and The Temple House.
4. The water provided by the hotel is placed on each floor for guests to use at will. This is a thumbs up. Sometimes it is troublesome to call the waiter to deliver water.

Let‚Äôs talk about dissatisfaction
1. We booked more than 1,000 yuan per night, and the daily cost is 7800 to 810 yuan per night. We also advertised the Atour high-end brand. The mouthwash cup was accidentally broken by a child. The first reaction was to remind us to pay compensation, and the second was to make arrangements. People will handle it. This kind of low-quality glass customized by the hotel and looking not upscale requires compensation because there is a problem with the hotel system. The reaction and attitude of the front desk is a problem with the company's customer service training. In addition, when checking in, the front desk did not mention the cultural tourism gifts, dining coupons and late-night snack services. Is it because the service was discounted because it was booked through a third-party platform? Finally, I suddenly remembered to ask for the cultural travel gift from the front desk when I checked out.
2. The lighting button settings in the room are very unreasonable. The bathroom switch button controls the lights in the bathroom and entrance as well as the lights on the water bar. If you have a child like me, turning on the light in the toilet will wake the child up.
3. The water retaining ***** in the shower room will cause a pool of water to flow to the floor at the door every time you take a shower. I don‚Äôt know how it was designed, and the carpet at the door cannot be placed, which is very unreasonable.

People say that after staying at Atour S, they will fall into Atour's trap, but I beg to differ. The location of this store is first-class. Although the hardware is not too old, there is a lot of room for improvement. The service is also commendable. p.s. The design of the laundry room upstairs is good, but three washing machines and one dryer are not enough. It is recommended to add a dryer.
